1.1.1 Ikke-tekstlig innhold (1 avvik)
Testregel 1.1.1a (1.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

SVG is missing accessible name

<svg class="boostAiChatButtonEnabled__svg" height="65" viewbox="0 0 69 65" width="69" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink"> <defs> <clippath id="a" transform="
Add <title> element inside SVG, or aria-label attribute. Use role='presentation' if decorative
1.3.1 Informasjon og relasjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

First heading is h2, should start with h1

<h2 class="mega-menu__heading">Utdanning og karriere</h2>
Start your heading structure with h1

2.4.3 Fokusrekkefølge (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.3 (2.4.3 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Positive tabindex (1) disrupts natural focus order

<a class="skip-link" href="#main-content" tabindex="1"> <div class="l-container--full">Hopp til innhald</div> </a>
Use tabindex='0' for focusable elements or '-1' for programmatic focus only
4.1.2 Navn, rolle, verdi (21 avvik)
Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

iframe is missing title attribute

<iframe height="0" src="//www.googletagmanager.com/ns.html?id=GTM-WVGJPVP" style="display: none; visibility: hidden" width="0"></iframe>
Add descriptive title attribute to iframe
Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Element with role='img' needs an accessible name

<span class="masthead__icon-search" role="img"> <span class="u-hidden">Åpne/lukk søk</span> </span>
Add aria-label or aria-labelledby attribute
Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Element with role='img' needs an accessible name

<span class="masthead__icon-hamburger" role="img"> <span class="u-hidden">Åpne/lukk meny</span> </span>
Add aria-label or aria-labelledby attribute
Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

2.4.2 Sidetittel (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.2 (2.4.2 - Nivå AA)
SERIOUS

Page is missing h1 heading

<body class="body l-site"> <!-- Google Tag Manager --> <noscript> <iframe height="0" src="//www.googletagmanager.com/ns.html?id=GTM-WVGJPVP" style="display: none; visibility: hidden" width="0"></ifram
Add a single h1 heading that describes the page content

Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Multiple nav elements exist but this one has no label

<nav class="breadcrumbs"> <a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/">Startside</a> <span>Nyheitsarkiv</span> </nav>
Add aria-label to distinguish between navigation regions (e.g., 'Main navigation', 'Footer navigation')
